GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*log(Abs(v) + c0) - beta*sin(v) - c1*beta*v - mu*(c2 - x**c3)*v
Candidate formulas: 50

GT (fixed) is
\[
-0.118064015949952\,v(1-x^2)\;-\;1.0053422414757\,v\;-\;0.502671120737851\log(|v|+1)\;+\;0.342318903764293\sin(t)\;-\;0.502671120737851\sin(v).
\]
Key required structures:
- a **pure** \(\sin(t)\) term (no \(x\)-dependent amplitude, no exp-of-sin, etc.)
- both \(\log(|v|+1)\) and \(\sin(v)\) (non-polynomial in \(v\))
- \(v(1-x^2)=v - v x^2\) cross-term: needs both a \(v\) term and a \(v x^2\) term with linked coefficients (but candidates may have \(v x^2\) explicitly)
- no other dependence (no \(x\)-only polynomials, no \(v^3\), no \(e^{(\cdot)}\) terms, etc.), unless their coefficients can be set to 0.

Now check each candidate for whether it can be tuned (and possibly under a plausible domain restriction) to exactly the GT.

1) Polynomial in \(x\) + \(x^2 e^{c t}\) + \(e^{\sin(\cdot)}\). No \(v\), no \(\log(|v|+1)\), no \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

2) Has \(v^3\), \(v\), \(e^{\sin(t)}\), and \(v x^2\). Missing \(\log(|v|+1)\) and \(\sin(v)\). Also \(e^{\sin(\cdot)}\) cannot become \(\sin(t)\) for all \(t\). Cannot match.

3) Has \(e^{c x}\), \(v^3\), \(v\), and \(\sin(\text{affine }t)\). Missing \(\log(|v|+1)\) and \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

4) \(x\)-polynomial + \(\cos(\text{affine }t)\) + linear \(v\). Can phase-shift cos to sin(t), but still missing \(\log(|v|+1)\) and \(\sin(v)\) and the \(v x^2\) term. Cannot match.

5) \(x\)-polynomial + \(x^2 e^{c t}\) + \(\cos(\text{affine }t)\). No \(v\), no log, no \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

6) \(e^{c x}\) + \(v e^{c|v|}\) + \(v|v|\) + \(e^{\sin(t)}\). GT needs \(\log(|v|+1)\) and \(\sin(v)\) and linear-in-\(v\) and \(v x^2\). None available; also \(e^{\sin}\neq \sin\). Cannot match.

7) Rational in \(x\) + \(e^{|v|}\cos(\cdot)\) + \(e^{|v|}\cos(t)\). No \(\log(|v|+1)\), no \(\sin(v)\), and wrong \(t\)-dependence (cos with exp(|v|) amplitude). Cannot match.

8) Linear in \(x\) + linear \(v\) + \(e^{c x}\sin(\text{affine }t)\) + \(v^{c}x^2\) + \(x^3\). Could set many to 0, but still cannot produce \(\log(|v|+1)\) or \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

9) \(x\)-polynomial + \(v\) + \(v x^2\) + \(e^{t}\cos(\text{affine }t)\). Has the needed \(v\) and \(v x^2\) shapes, but **no** \(\log(|v|+1)\) and **no** \(\sin(v)\). Also \(t\)-term is \(e^{c t}\cos(\cdot)\), cannot equal pure \(\sin(t)\) for all \(t\) unless coefficient 0 (then you lose \(\sin(t)\)). Cannot match.

10) Linear \(x\) + linear \(v\) + \(e^{c x}\sin(\text{affine }t)\) + \(v x^2\). Missing \(\log(|v|+1)\) and \(\sin(v)\). Also \(\sin(t)\) term would be multiplied by \(e^{c x}\); to make amplitude independent of \(x\) you’d need \(c4=0\) so \(e^{0}=1\), that part is fine, but still missing log and \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

11) Linear \(x\) + \(v\sin(\text{affine }t)\) + \(e^{t}\sin(\cdot)\) + linear \(v\). Missing \(\log(|v|+1)\), \(\sin(v)\), and \(v x^2\). Cannot match.

12) \(x\)-polynomial + \(e^{\cos(\text{affine in }x,t)}\). No \(v\), no log, no \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

13) \(x\)-polynomial + \(v\) + \(x^5\) + \(\sin(\text{affine }t)\). Missing \(\log(|v|+1)\), \(\sin(v)\), and \(v x^2\). Cannot match.

14) Same as 13 but cos. Same issues. Cannot match.

15) \(x\)-polynomial + \(v x^2\) + \(\sin(\text{affine }t)\) + linear \(v\) + \(x^5\). You can zero out \(x\)-only terms and match \(\sin(t)\) via phase/scale, and match linear \(v\) and \(v x^2\). But still **no** \(\log(|v|+1)\) and **no** \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

16) Rational + \(x^3\) + \(\log(|x|)\sin(t)\) + \(\cos(t)\). Log is in \(|x|\), not \(|v|\). No \(\sin(v)\), no linear \(v\) or \(v x^2\). Cannot match.

18) Linear \(x\) + \(v\sin(\text{affine }t)\) + \(e^{c v}\cos(\text{affine }t)\). No \(\log(|v|+1)\), no \(\sin(v)\), no \(v x^2\). Cannot match.

19) \(x\)-polynomial + \(e^{t}\cos(t)\). No \(v\), no log, no \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

20) Linear \(x\) + \(v x^2\) + \(\log(c e^{c x}+1)\) + linear \(v\) + \(\sin(\text{affine }t)\). Log is a function of \(x\), not \(|v|\). No \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

21) \(x\)-polynomial + \(v\) + \(e^{c x}\sin(\text{affine }t)\). No \(v x^2\), no \(\log(|v|+1)\), no \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

22) \(x\)-polynomial + \(v^3\) + \(\sin(\text{affine }t)\) + linear \(v\). Missing \(\log(|v|+1)\), \(\sin(v)\), and \(v x^2\). Cannot match.

23) Like 9 but with \(e^{\sin(t)}\) instead of \(e^{t}\cos\). Still missing \(\log(|v|+1)\) and \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

24) Linear/quadratic in \(x\) with \(x\cos(\cdot)\) + \(e^{c x}\cos(t)\). No \(v\), no log, no \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

25) \(x\)-polynomial + \(\sin(\text{affine }t)\) + \(\log(c x^2 e^{c t}+1)\). Log depends on \(x,t\), not \(|v|\). No \(v\) terms at all, no \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

26) Same structure as 15. Still no \(\log(|v|+1)\) and no \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

27) \(e^{1/(c+x)} + x^5 + \sin(\cos(e^{t}))\). No \(v\), no log, no \(\sin(v)\), wrong \(t\). Cannot match.

28) \(e^{1/(c+x)} + x^5 + v|v| + \sin(\log((c v+t)^2+1))\). Has \(v|v|\) not linear \(v\), no \(\log(|v|+1)\), no \(\sin(v)\), no \(v x^2\), and \(t\) appears inside a log inside sin. Cannot match.

29) \(x\)-polynomial + \(e^{\sin(t)}\). No \(v\), no \(\log(|v|+1)\), no \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

30) \(x\)-polynomial + \(v\) + \(e^{\sin(t)}\). Missing \(v x^2\), \(\log(|v|+1)\), \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

31) \(x\)-polynomial + \(\cos(c e^{t}+c x)\). No \(v\), no log, no \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

32) \(x\)-polynomial + \(x|x|\) + \(v/(c+|v|)\) + \(\sin(\text{affine }t)\). Still no \(\log(|v|+1)\), no \(\sin(v)\), no \(v x^2\). Cannot match.

33) \(e^{c x} + e^{c x}\cos(t) + x\). No \(v\), no log, no \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

34) \(x e^{c x} + e^{c x}\cos(t) + \cos(t)\). No \(v\), no log, no \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

35) Rational in \(x\) + \(\cos(t)\) + \(e^{t}\cos(t)\). No \(v\), no log, no \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

36) \(e^{c x} + v + v x^2 + e^{c x}\sin(t) + x + x^3\). Has \(v\) and \(v x^2\), and can make \(e^{c x}\sin(\cdot)\) into pure \(\sin(t)\) by setting that exponent coefficient to 0 and phase-shifting. But still **no** \(\log(|v|+1)\) and **no** \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

37) Sum of exponentials in \(x\) and \(e^{c x}\cos(t)\). No \(v\), no log, no \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

38) Exponentials in \(x\) + \(e^{c x}\cos(t)\) + \(\sin(c e^{c x}+c)\). No \(v\), no log, no \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

39) Exponentials in \(x\) + \(e^{c x}\cos(t)\) + \(v^3\) + \(v\sin(\text{affine }t)\). Missing \(\log(|v|+1)\), \(\sin(v)\), and \(v x^2\). Cannot match.

40) Rational in \(x\) + \(\log(c|v|+1)\sin(\text{affine }t)\) + \(\cos(t)\). This has a \(\log(|v|+1)\)-like factor, but it is **multiplied by \(\sin(t)\)**, whereas GT has \(\log(|v|+1)\) as a standalone term and \(\sin(t)\) standalone. There is no way to separate the product into a sum for all \(t,v\) by choosing constants, except setting the product coefficient to 0 (then you lose the log term entirely). Also no \(\sin(v)\), no linear \(v\) or \(v x^2\). Cannot match.

41) Linear \(x\) + \(v\sin(\text{affine }t)\) + \(e^{t}\sin(\cdot)\). No \(\log(|v|+1)\), no \(\sin(v)\), no \(v x^2\). Cannot match.

42) Rational in \(x\) + \(e^{|v|}\cos(\cdot)\) + \(e^{\sin(t)}\). No \(\log(|v|+1)\), no \(\sin(v)\), no linear \(v\) or \(v x^2\). Cannot match.

43) Linear \(x\) + \(v\sin(\text{affine }t)\) + \(e^{c v}\cos(t)\) + \(x^5\). No \(\log(|v|+1)\), no \(\sin(v)\), no \(v x^2\). Cannot match.

44) Linear \(x\) + \(\cos(e^{t})\) + \(v x^2\) + \(v x\). Missing \(\log(|v|+1)\), \(\sin(v)\), and pure \(\sin(t)\). Cannot match.

45) \(e^{c x} + \text{const} + e^{c x}\cos(t)\). No \(v\), no log, no \(\sin(v)\). Cannot match.

46) Linear \(x\) + \(v^3\) and \(v\) terms + \(e^{t}\cos(t)\). Missing \(\log(|v|+1)\), \(\sin(v)\), and \(v x^2\); also wrong \(t\)-term. Cannot match.

47) Linear \(x\) + \(\cos(e^{t})\) + \(v\cos(c x)\). Missing \(\log(|v|+1)\), \(\sin(v)\), \(v x^2\), and \(\sin(t)\). Cannot match.

48) \(x e^{c x} + v^3 + \cos(t)\). Missing \(\log(|v|+1)\), \(\sin(v)\), linear \(v\), \(v x^2\). Cannot match.

49) Rational in \(x\) + \(\cos(t)\) + \(x^5\) + \(\log(\sin(\text{affine in }x,v)+1)\). Log is of \(\sin(\cdot)\), not \(|v|+1\); also no \(\sin(v)\), no linear \(v\), no \(v x^2\), and \(t\)-term is cos not necessarily an issue (phase shift), but other mismatches remain. Cannot match.

50) Linear \(x\) + \(\cos(e^{t})\) + \(v\log(x^2+1)\). Missing \(\log(|v|+1)\) (log is in \(x\)), missing \(\sin(v)\), missing correct \(v(1-x^2)\) structure (has \(v\log(\cdot)\) instead). Cannot match.

Conclusion: none of the candidates contain (or can be tuned to produce) the essential standalone \(-\beta\log(|v|+1)\) and \(-\beta\sin(v)\) terms simultaneously, along with the required linear \(v\) and \(v x^2\) structure and a pure \(\sin(t)\) term.

Simplifying: `0.118064*v*x² - 1.12340*v - 0.502671*log(|v| + 1) + 0.342319*sin(t) - 0.502671*sin(v)`

The GT has these basis functions:
1. `v*x²` (linear in v, quadratic in x)
2. `v` (linear)
3. `log(|v| + 1)` (nonlinear in v)
4. `sin(t)` (sinusoidal in t)
5. `sin(v)` (sinusoidal in v)

Let me check each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** `c0*x³ + c1*x² + c2*x + c3 + c4*x²*exp(c5*t) + c6*exp(c7*sin(c8*t + c9))`
No `v` dependence at all. Cannot match GT which depends on `v`.
Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 2:** `c0 + c1*v³ + c2*v + c3*exp(c4*sin(c5*t + c6)) + c7*v*x²`
Has `v*x²`, `v`, and `exp(c4*sin(t))` terms. But GT needs `log(|v|+1)`, `sin(v)`, and `sin(t)`. The `v³` cannot replicate `log(|v|+1)` or `sin(v)`. The `exp(sin(t))` is not `sin(t)`.
Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 3:** `c0*exp(c1*x) + c2*v³ + c3*v + c4*sin(c5*t + c6)`
Has `sin(t)` and `v` terms but no `v*x²`, no `log(|v|+1)`, no `sin(v)`. `v³` can't replace these.
Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 4:** `c0*x + c1 + c2*v³ + c3*x + c4*x³ + c5*cos(c6*t + c7) + c8*v`
No `v*x²`, no `log(|v|+1)`, no `sin(v)`. Polynomial in x and v³ can't match.
Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 5:** `c0*x³ + c1*x² + c2*x + c3 + c4*x²*exp(c5*t) + c6*cos(c7*t + c8)`
No `v` dependence.

Candidate 8 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 9:** `c0*x³ + c1*x² + c2*v + c3*v*x² + c4*x + c5 + c6*exp(c7*t)*cos(c8*t+c9)`

**Candidate 10:** `c0*x + c1 + c2*v + c3*exp(c4*x)*sin(c5*t+c6) + c7*v*x²`
Has `v*x²`, `v`, but `exp(x)*sin(t)` couples x and t. Missing `log(|v|+1)`, `sin(v)`.
Candidate 10 verdict: [NO MATCH]
